#Coring Decisions

DEBUG_Coring_Decisions = {

DEBUG_Core_Everything = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 0
		modifier = { }

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
		
	}

}

#Greater Germany
GER_Coring_Decisions = {

	#Easy German Cores

	#Free City of Danzig
	GER_Core_Danzig = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			85 = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			85 = { NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			85 = {
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	#Sudetenland
	GER_Core_Sudetenland = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = CZE
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = CZE
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

			modifier = {

				}
			}

						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }

							state = 100
							state = 101
							state = 337
							state = 912
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {

	#Greater Germanic Reich
	RON_Formable_Decision1 = {
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		cost = 10
		days_re_enable = 0
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = FORM_GGR2 }
			original_tag = GER
		}
		available = {
			#is_subject = no
			
			has_global_flag = FORM_GRO2
			has_government = fascism
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_POL_Neutralized_tt
				OR = {
					POL = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
					POL = {
						exists = no
					}
					POL = {
						is_subject_of = GER
					}
					OR = {
						GER = {
							controls_state = 10
						}
						any_other_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_FRA_Neutralized_tt
				
				OR = {
					FRA = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
					FRA = {
						exists = no
					}
					FRA = {
						is_subject_of = GER
					}
					OR = {
						GER = {
							controls_state = 16
						}
						any_other_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							controls_state = 16
						}
					}
					has_global_flag = fall_of_france
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_SOV_Neutralized_tt
				OR = {
						SOV = {
							has_capitulated = yes
						}
						SOV = {
							exists = no
						}
						SOV = {
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
						AND = {
							OR = {
								GER = {
									controls_state = 219
								}
								any_other_country = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
									controls_state = 219
								}
							}
							OR = {
								GER = {
									controls_state = 217
								}
								any_other_country = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
									controls_state = 217
								}
							}
							OR = {
								GER = {
									controls_state = 195
								}
								any_other_country = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
									controls_state = 195
								}
							}
						}
					}
			}
			
			
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_German_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = GER
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Austrian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = AUS
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			#Polish Corridor
			85 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			86 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			807 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			762 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }

			#Memel
			188 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }

			#Alsace
			28 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			
			#Northern Sleswig
			912 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			
			#Sudetenland
			69 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			74 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {

				id = RON_Formable_Country.1

#French Empire
FRA_Coring_Decisions = {

	#Luxembourg
	FRA_Core_Luxembourg = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4	
			8 = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			8 = { NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			8 = {
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	#Quebec
	FRA_Core_Quebec = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 40
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 10 }
		days_remove = 14

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 9	
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = CAN
						#No land link possible
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM
						#}
						OR = {
							state = 466
							state = 860
							state = 861
							state = 862
							state = 863
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {

			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							state = 466
							state = 860
							state = 861
							state = 862
							state = 863
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = CAN
						#No land link possible
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM
						#}
						OR = {
							state = 466
							state = 860
							state = 861
							state = 862
							state = 863
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	#Whole Ireland
	ENG_Core_Ireland = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

						}

							is_core_of = CAN
							is_island_state = no
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Australian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = AST
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_New_Zealand_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = NZL
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_American_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = USA
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}

		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RON_Formable_Country.89
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = FORM_Anglosphere2
			}
		}
	}

#Whole Canada
	USA_Core_Canada = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = CAN
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = {
								is_core_of = FROM
							}
							state = 331
							state = 739
							state = 740
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = CAN
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = CAN
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = {
								is_core_of = FROM
							}
							state = 331
							state = 739
							state = 740
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

		days_remove = 21

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 14
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = DOM
							is_core_of = HAI
						}
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM
						#}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = DOM
							is_core_of = HAI
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = DOM
							is_core_of = HAI
						}
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM

				}

			}

		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 60
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 15 }
		days_remove = 21

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = FORM_WROE2
				has_global_flag = FORM_ROE2
			}
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 14
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SPR
							state = 118
						}
						NOT = { state = 177 }
						NOT = { state = 178 }
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SPR
							state = 118
						}
						NOT = { state = 177 }
						NOT = { state = 178 }
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SPR
							state = 118
						}
						NOT = { state = 177 }
						NOT = { state = 178 }
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

#Greater Japan
JAP_Coring_Decisions = {

#Whole Taiwan
	JAP_Core_Taiwan = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						state = 524
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM
						#}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						state = 524
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						state = 524
						#any_neighbor_state = {
						#	is_core_of = FROM
						#}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = DEN
						OR = {
							any_neighbor_state = {
								is_core_of = FROM
							}
							state = 910
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 100
							state = 101
							state = 337
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

							state = 66
							state = 67

#Sudetenland
	AUS_Core_Sudetenland = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = CZE
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = CZE
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	#South Tyrol
	AUS_Core_South_Tyrol = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			39 = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			39 = { NOT = { is_core_of = FROM } }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			39 = {
				add_core_of = FROM
				set_state_name = "Südtirol"
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	#Austro Hungarian Cores
	
	#Greater Austria will be added as its own separate category
	#Greater Austria
	RON_Formable_Decision107 = {
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		cost = 10
		days_re_enable = 0
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = Form_Greater_Austria2 }
			original_tag = AUS
		}
		available = {
			#is_subject = no
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Austrian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = AUS
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Czech_States_tt
				69 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
				74 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
				9 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
				75 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Slovene_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SLV
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}

		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RON_Formable_Country.107
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = Form_Greater_Austria2
			}
		}
	}

}

AUH_Core_Austria = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {

					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }

					}
				}

		}

		}
		
		remove_effect = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 60
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 15 }
		days_remove = 21

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		has_global_flag = FORM_BAK2	
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 14
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = ROM
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = ROM
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = ROM
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

							state = 797

						OR = {
							state = 341
							state = 797
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }

	#Greater Croatia
	RON_Formable_Decision60 = {
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		cost = 10
		days_re_enable = 0
		allowed = {
			original_tag = CRO
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = FORM_GCR2 }
		}
		available = {
			#is_subject = no
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Croatian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = CRO
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Bosnian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = BOS
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RON_Formable_Country.60
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = FORM_GCR2
			}
		}
	}

			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }

				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = PER
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}

ARG_Coring_Decisions = {

#Whole Argentina
	ARG_Core_Argentina = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = ARG
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						is_core_of = ARG
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						is_core_of = ARG
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 60
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 15 }
		days_remove = 21

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 14
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						state = 655
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						state = 655
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						state = 655
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

	RON_Formable_Decision5 = {
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		cost = 10
		days_re_enable = 0
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = FORM_QIN2 }
		}
		available = {
			#is_subject = no
			
			#Chinese
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Chinese_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = CHI
							NOT = { state = 728 }
							NOT = { state = 729 }
							NOT = { state = 326 }
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			#Mongolia
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Mongolian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = MON
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			#Tannu Tuva
			329 = { is_controlled_by = FROM }
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Tibetan_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = TIB
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RON_Formable_Country.5
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = FORM_QIN2
			}
		}
	}

					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Bolivian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = BOL
							NOT = { is_core_of = PAR }
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RON_Controls_Ecuadorian_States_tt
				all_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = ECU
							NOT = { state = 649 }
						}
						is_controlled_by = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
		icon = generic_form_nation
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RON_Formable_Country.100
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = FORM_Greater_Peru2
			}
		}
	}

SAF_Coring_Decisions = {

#Border States
	SAF_Core_Border_States = {

		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		#Allow Multiple Times as it cores States one by one
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 20
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 5 }
		days_remove = 7

		allowed = {
			
		}

		available = {
		num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			any_controlled_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = BOT
							is_core_of = ZIM
							state = 544
							state = 896
						}
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			
			any_state = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = BOT
							is_core_of = ZIM
							state = 544
							state = 896
						}
					}
				}

		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_ai = no } hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus } }
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {		
					AND = {
						NOT = {is_core_of = FROM}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = BOT
							is_core_of = ZIM
							state = 544
							state = 896
						}
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
			clr_country_flag = Coring_In_Progress
		}
	}

}
